### Feature Coverage Details

#### v2.1.168

- **[covered]** - Bug fixes and reliability improvements
  - Covered by: `cc-native/agents-skills/CC-skills-adoption-analysis.md`

#### v2.1.167

- **[covered]** - Bug fixes and reliability improvements
  - Covered by: `cc-native/agents-skills/CC-skills-adoption-analysis.md`

#### v2.1.166

- **[covered]** - Added `fallbackModel` setting to configure up to three fallback models tried in order when the primary model is overloaded or unavailable; `--fallback-model` now also applies to interactive sessions
  - Covered by: `cc-native/agents-skills/CC-agent-teams-orchestration.md`, `cc-native/agents-skills/CC-plans-as-skill-rule-templates.md`, `cc-native/ci-remote/CC-cloud-sessions-analysis.md`
- **[covered]** - Added glob pattern support in deny rule tool-name position (`"*"` denies all tools); allow rules reject non-MCP globs, and unknown tool names in deny rules warn at startup
  - Covered by: `cc-native/agents-skills/CC-agent-teams-orchestration.md`, `cc-native/agents-skills/CC-agentic-harness-patterns-analysis.md`, `cc-native/agents-skills/CC-cli-anything-analysis.md`
- **[covered]** - Hardened cross-session messaging: messages relayed via `SendMessage` from other Claude sessions no longer carry user authority — receivers refuse relayed permission requests, and auto mode blocks them
  - Covered by: `cc-native/CC-first-party-docs-index.md`, `cc-native/agents-skills/CC-agent-teams-orchestration.md`, `cc-native/agents-skills/CC-plans-as-skill-rule-templates.md`
- **[covered]** - `MAX_THINKING_TOKENS=0`, `--thinking disabled`, and the per-model thinking toggle now disable thinking on models that think by default via the Claude API (3P providers unchanged)
  - Covered by: `cc-native/CC-first-party-docs-index.md`, `cc-native/agents-skills/CC-skills-adoption-analysis.md`, `cc-native/ci-remote/CC-cloud-sessions-analysis.md`
- **[covered]** - Claude Code now retries a turn once on the fallback model when the API rejects an unexpected non-retryable error; auth, rate-limit, request-size, and transport errors still surface immediately
  - Covered by: `cc-native/CC-first-party-docs-index.md`, `cc-native/agents-skills/CC-agent-teams-orchestration.md`, `cc-native/agents-skills/CC-plans-as-skill-rule-templates.md`
- **[covered]** - `claude update` now announces the target version before downloading instead of going silent
  - Covered by: `cc-native/CC-first-party-docs-index.md`, `cc-native/agents-skills/CC-skills-adoption-analysis.md`, `cc-native/ci-remote/CC-cloud-sessions-analysis.md`
- **[covered]** - `claude agents`: typing a URL into the list now filters to the session whose first prompt contained it
  - Covered by: `cc-native/CC-first-party-docs-index.md`, `cc-native/agents-skills/CC-recursive-spawning-patterns.md`, `cc-native/agents-skills/CC-skills-adoption-analysis.md`
- **[covered]** - Fixed a recurring "image could not be processed" error and extra token usage when an unprocessable image was sent in a session
  - Covered by: `cc-native/agents-skills/CC-agent-teams-orchestration.md`, `cc-native/agents-skills/CC-plans-as-skill-rule-templates.md`, `cc-native/agents-skills/CC-recursive-spawning-patterns.md`
- **[covered]** - Fixed remote sessions becoming permanently stuck when a brief backend disruption occurred during worker registration at startup
  - Covered by: `cc-native/agents-skills/CC-agent-teams-orchestration.md`, `cc-native/agents-skills/CC-cli-anything-analysis.md`, `cc-native/agents-skills/CC-plans-as-skill-rule-templates.md`
- **[covered]** - Fixed flickering in JetBrains IDE terminals (IntelliJ, PyCharm, WebStorm, etc.) on 2026.1+ by enabling synchronized output
  - Covered by: `cc-native/configuration/CC-cli-reference.md`, `cc-native/configuration/CC-inline-visuals-analysis.md`, `cc-native/configuration/CC-model-provider-configuration.md`
- **[covered]** - Fixed Shift+non-ASCII characters (e.g. Shift+ä → Ä) being dropped in terminals using the Kitty keyboard protocol (WezTerm, Ghostty, kitty)
  - Covered by: `cc-native/ci-remote/CC-version-pinning-resilience.md`, `cc-native/ci-remote/CC-web-auth-setup-analysis.md`, `cc-native/plugins-ecosystem/CC-web-scraping-plugins-analysis.md`
- **[covered]** - Fixed PowerShell command validation occasionally hanging far past its time budget on Windows when a killed process's children held its output pipes

- **[covered]** - Fixed orphaned `claude --bg-pty-host` processes spinning at 100% CPU after the daemon dies while connected on macOS
  - Covered by: `cc-native/CC-first-party-docs-index.md`, `cc-native/agents-skills/CC-plans-as-skill-rule-templates.md`, `cc-native/agents-skills/CC-skills-adoption-analysis.md`

  - Covered by: `cc-native/CC-first-party-docs-index.md`, `cc-native/agents-skills/CC-agent-teams-orchestration.md`, `cc-native/agents-skills/CC-cli-anything-analysis.md`

- **[covered]** - Added `requiredMinimumVersion` and `requiredMaximumVersion` managed settings — Claude Code refuses to start if its version is outside the allowed range and directs the user to an approved version

- **[covered]** - Hooks: Stop and SubagentStop hooks can now return `hookSpecificOutput.additionalContext` to give Claude feedback and keep the turn going without being labeled a hook error

- **[covered]** - stdio MCP servers now receive the same `CLAUDE_CODE_SESSION_ID` as hooks/Bash on `--resume`

- **[covered]** - Fixed `claude -p` hanging forever after its final result when a backgrounded command never exits — background shells are now stopped ~5s after the result once stdin closes

- **[covered]** - Fixed bash commands failing under bazel and EDR-protected Go workflows: `$TMPDIR` was overridden to `/tmp/claude-{uid}` for all commands instead of only sandboxed ones (regression in 2.1.154)

- **[covered]** - Added `worktree.baseRef` setting (`fresh` | `head`) to choose whether `--worktree`, `EnterWorktree`, and agent-isolation worktrees branch from `origin/<default>` or local `HEAD`. **Note:** the default `fresh` changes `EnterWorktree`'s base back to `origin/<default>` (it has been local `HEAD` since 2.1.128) — set `worktree.baseRef: "head"` to keep unpushed commits in new worktrees
